 saste gharon ke nirmaan ke liye jahaan bilderon ko or zyada aage aane kii jarurat he, vahiin sarkaar ko bhi kifayati gharon ke nirmaan ko protsaahan dene kii jarurat he
 In the coming years, in view of the pace with which urbanization is increasing in the country, lakhs of crores of people will move to cities in search of better life from rural areas
 yojana ayog kii report ke mutabik 2031 tak desh ke shaharon main aabaadi 60 karod tak ho chuki hogi, jo ki 2011 ke mukaable 59 fisadi zyada hogi
 In such a situation, affordable houses are the need of the hour, so it is possible to earn profits if the builders reduce the expectation of huge profit margins
 jaankaron kaa maananaa he ki yah lambey daur ke liye aakarshak bijness niti ho sakati he, jahaan munafa har unit se nahin uniton kii sankhya se tay hoga

 kuch kaa kahana he ki ye hyper tension main phydemand rahati he or kuch kaa kahana he ki ise niyamit pine se madhumeh kii samasya main phayda hota he
 If all these claims are put aside, then a big question is whether green tea is really beneficial in losing weight? There is no doubt that drinking green tea is more than drinking coffee
 Is beneficial
 iskaa sabase bada kaaran ye he ki isamen paryaapt maatra main anti-oxident hote hai
 Green tea contains vitamin A, B, B5, D, E, C, k and H
 iske alaava isamen selenium, chromium, zinc, caffeine or maiganej bhi paryaapt maatra main hote hai
 An element named EGCG is also found in it
 hamaara sharir prakritik rup se taapmaana vruddhi karata he
 It is a part of the process of heat metabolism
 aise main jab aap ek cap green tii pite hai to sharir kaa taapmaana kuch bad jaataa he
 Increase in temperature directly means more calories will be burnt and more calories burnt means less weight
 green tii metabolism kii prakriya ko or adhik sakriy kar detaa he
 The element named EGCG present in green tea is responsible for this process
 caffeine kii matraaisa nahin he ki green tii main caffeine kii maatra nahin hoti
 One cup of green tea contains about 30 mg of caffeine
 iske istemaal se sakriyata bad jaati he ouriskaa sidhaa asar kaam par najar aata he
 In such a situation, it is proved that the use of green tea reduces weight, but it is not right to use green tea only to lose weight or just to rely on it

 china ne samjhaute kii gunjaaish se inkaar karne ke baad ab bharat ko sabak sikhaane kii dhamkee di he
 On Wednesday, China's official newspaper Global Times said that the time has come to teach India a lesson once again
 is baar bharat kaa 1962 se bhi zyada bura haal karne kaa samay aa gaya he
 Following the statement by Defense Minister Arun Jaitley, such a sharp comment from the Chinese newspaper has been seen
 darasal, sikkim sector par tanaav ke baad china ne bharat ko 1962 kii haar kii yaad dilaai thi, jiske jawaab main raksha mantri jetali ne kaha tha ki 1962 se ab ke halaat alag hai
 India should not forget to understand the country of 1962
 1962 ke bharat or 2017 ke bharat main antar he
 Earlier, Army Chief Bipin Rawat had said that India is ready to fight a war with China and Pakistan simultaneously
 isse baukhalaaye chini akhbaar kii yah kadi pratikriya di he
 The Chinese newspaper said that if India thinks that it can use the army in Donglong area and is ready for a simultaneous war against China and Pakistan, then we have to tell India that it can reduce the strength of the Chinese army Is taking in global times ne apane sampadakeey main likhaa ki jetali thik kah rahe hai ki 1962 or 2017 ke bharat main kaaphi antar he, lekin agar jang hui, to bharat ko zyada nuksaan uthaanaa hoga
 China believes that if the tension in Donglong area is to end, the Indian Army will have to retreat
 varanaa chini sainik karrwai karenge
 China is blaming the Indian army for infiltration
 chini akhbaar kii pratikriya se ek baat to saaf he ki china bharat ke saath jang ke mood main he
 The newspaper said that China is building a road in the Doklam area, which India is instigating Bhutan to oppose
 uskaa kahana he ki bharat kaa makasad china ke donglong ilaake ko vivaadit kshetra main tabdeel karnaa he or chini nirmaan kaary ko rokna he
 The Chinese newspaper said that India should first see the mirror
 uske paas chini sainikon ke ghuspaith ke saboot nahin hai
 In addition, Yang Siling newspaper of China said that India is provoking Bhutan to protest against China
 maaloom ho ki chini sena ne dokalam ilaake main ghuspaith kii thi or do bunker tainaat kar die the

 website contactmusic

 meri daadi mujhe is tarah sone ke liye prerit karti hai'
